The feature is that each room has a large terrace, floor-to-ceiling windows, and an intelligent system. The most unexpected thing this time was the service. I received a call on the way here, which made me think I met a scammerü§•. When I arrived at the hotel, I found that it was really the customer service. I took the initiative to add WeChat, which was convenient for contact and problem solving. The service was very good throughout the whole process, which was obviously different from the last time I came. Last time, basically no one paid attention to you. I asked the customer service and said that the boss went to experience the hotel in the south and came back to make requirements for everyone. I was so kind that I had to give a thumbs upüëç. The design of the hotel is also a plus. The sun room area in the middle surrounded by the buildings on both sides has both indoor warmth and outdoor freshness, and is also decorated with many green plants. A new children's leisure area has been opened in the middle. I feel that it would be better if it were free to play, after all, the consumables are not expensive. And the space is a bit cramped after adding the leisure area. The price of 700 is a bit expensive. The outdoor mountain is not open. It should be full of green in summer, which is even more beautiful! I also like the breakfast, which is quite rich. Well, I didn't find the leisure area on the second floor at first, but after a round, I found that there were not many people. Overall, it's good. Such beautiful hardware coupled with humanized service has room for development!
